na laman na tapi ta diad sayan laman so aponiti ed kinen jacob
anengneng nen jacob si esau a nitan lan kaiba to ray apat a lasus a totoo to kanyan inapag to ray ogogaw ed kindi lea raquel tan saramay duaran bibiin aripen to walad onaan ira may aripen tan saray anak da insan mantombuk si lea tan saray anak to tan diad onur si raquel tan si jose inmonay jacob ed sikaran amin tan nandakmomon amimpito legan ya onaasingger ed kinen agi to balet binatik nen esau ya inabet nilakap to insan to inanguban manakis iran dua nen anengneng nen esau ira may bibii tan saramay ogogaw tinepet to siopa ra yay kaibam inmebat si jacob sikara yay ogogaw ya inter na dios ed siak lapud panangaro to inmasingger ira may aripen tan saramay anak da tan dinmakmomo ran angigalang sinmoblay si lea tan saramay anak to tan say kaonuran si jose tan si raquel tinepet nen esau antoy kabaliksan da ra may onaan a nabet ko inmebat si jacob rigalok ira man ed sika ta labay koy mipulangan ed sika balet inkuanen esau malaem la ray kayaryan ko agi kien mo la ray kayaryan mo inkuanen jacob andi komun no talagan pirdonaen mo ak awat moy panangarok say pakanengneng kod lupam et singa pakanengneng kod lupa na dios natan ta maung so impatnag mod siak awat mo kariy panangarok ya awit kon para sika kinasian ak na dios ta inter ton amin iray nakaukolan ko ag to tinondaan ya anggad inawat nen esau ira may rigalo inkuanen esau onla itayo la siak so onona inmebat si jacob naksawan tan makapoy la ra yay ogogaw insan sakey ni nakaukolan ya asikasoen ko ra yay karniro tan baka tan saray kilaw da no dagdagen iran manakar a masiglat ed sanagew labat ompatey iran amin onona ka la ta ontombuk ak lan mantantan manakar kami onung na anggaay nayarian na saray ayayep tan saray ogogaw anggad naabot ta kad edom inkuanen esau no ontan sirin mangitilak ak ed sika na pigaran totook balet inkuanen jacob andibali la tan masarag lay impamirdonam ed siak kanyan diad saman ya agew amaarap lad edom si esau si jacob balet linmad sukot tan diman angipaalagey na dilin abung to tan saray salimbengan na ayayep to kanyan atawag na sukot iman a pasen nen ompawil si jacob a manlapud mesopotamia maliket ya akasabid sikem diad sakop na canaan tan nankampod sakey ya alog ya asingger ed siudad sinaliw to man a parti na alog ed saray kabyangay boleg nen hamor ya ama nen sikem sanlasus a kuartan pilak so imbayar to nanggawad may sakey ya altar tan nginaranan to para el say dios na israel
aminsan ya agew si dina a biin anak nen jacob tan lea et linman dinmalaw ed pigaran bibiid canaan nen anengneng nen sikem a lakin anak nen hamor a heveo imbatik to insan to pinasoot ya inakdulan balet nen naimano ton magangganan tuloy si dina sinmabiy baleg a panibeg tod sikato tan kinokoyung to inkuantod kinen ama to labay kon asawaen yan bii ala yo pa a para siak naamtaan nen jacob so impamasoot dad anak ton dina balet lapud saray anak ton lalaki et wala rad kaalogan anggapoy ginawa to ya anggad insabi ra nen nitan la ray lalakin anak nen jacob a nanlapud kaalogan sinmabi met si hamor ya ama nen sikem ta labay toy mitongtong ed kinen jacob nen nadngelan day agawa abigla ra tan mapalaloy pasnuk da ed sayan impamasoot nen sikem ed agi ran bii tan say impamaabeba tod saray totood israel inkuanen hamor ed sikara si anak kon sikem et naibegan toy anak mon marikit paasawam la kari ed sikato mampapaknaan tayo ya iyabuloy tayoy panaasawaan na totoo tayo diad ontan nayarian yoy manayam diad bansa mi nayarian yoy manayam ed inerman a labay yo mannigosio kayo tan mankayaryan kayo na antokaman insan inkuanen sikem ed kinen ama nen dina tan saray agagi ton lalaki iter yo yan kekerewen ko et iter koy antokaman a labay yo ibaga yod siak no anto ray labay yon irigalok tan no pigay labay yon ibayar ko iter koy antokaman a kerewen yo dapot no paasawa yod siak si dina saramay lalakin anak nen jacob et inebatan day marakep si sikem tan si ama to balet walad kanunotan dan palikdoen da ra lapud agawa ed kinen dina ya agi ra inkuandad kinen sikem ag mi iyabuloy a miasaway agi mi ed sakey a lakin ag asegat makapabaing yad sikami onabuloy kami labat no magmaliw kayon singa sikami diad pamasegat yod amin a lalaki ed sikayo onabuloy kami met a manaasawaan iray totoo mi tan saray totoo yo manayam kami dia tan mikasakey kamid sikayo balet no ag kayo onabubon ed saraya awiten miy dina tan ontaynan kami la inmabubon si hamor tan si anak ton si sikem ag la nanabalay sikem ya anumpal ed tongtongan da ta inaro to may biin anak nen jacob manona si sikem ed amin da ray kabyangay pamilya to linma si hamor tan si anak ton sikem ed pandaragupan na totoo diad puirtay baley tan inkuandad saray kabaleyan da makaaro ra yay totoon sinmabi diad sikatayo panayamen ti la ra dia tan paolyan ti ran mannigosio dia maawang met ingen yay lugar tayo asawaen ti ray mamarikit da tan ipaasawa tayo ray mamarikit tayo ed sikara balet manayam ira dia tan mikasakey irad sikatayo no pasegat tayon amin iray lalaki ed sikatayo a singa sikara diad onya nakayaryan tayoy amin ya ayayep da tan arum ni ran kayaryan da kanyan onabuloy ti lan manayam ira diad sikatayo inmabuloy ya amin iray ombaley ed imbaga di hamor tan sikem kanyan nampasegat ya amin iray lalaki kasumpal na taloy agew nen ag ni inmabig ira may nampasegat saray duaran lalakin anak nen jacob tan agagi nen dina a di simeon tan si levi et inala ray ispada ra linma rad siudad ya anggapoy makaamtad getma ra insan da pinatey ya amin iray lalaki pinatey da met si hamor tan si anak ton sikem inala ray dina ed abung nen sikem insan la ra tinmaynan kasumpal na impanpapatey nen simeon tan si levi sinmabi ray arum ya anak nen jacob tan inala ray amin a naala ra ed baley ginawa ra ya pian makabawi ra ed inkaderal na kagalangan na agi ra inala ray amin a karniro baka asno tan amin a bengatlan walad baley tan diad kaalogan inala ray amin a makana inala ra met iray bibii tan saray ogogaw tan amin a bengatlan walad kaabungan inkuanen jacob ed kindi simeon tan levi initdan yo ak na gunigon natan bosulen ak na saray cananeo saray perezeo tan amin iray wadyad sayan pasen dagdaiset iray totook no mankakasakey iran amin insan da ak labanan ompatey so intiron pamilya tayo balet inmebat ira ag nayarin gawaen dan singa marotak a bii si dina ya agi mi
inkuan na dios ed kinen jacob lakan tampol ed betel tan manayam kad man manggawa kad may altar a para siak a dios a pinmayawar ed sika nen ibabatikan moy agim ya esau kanyan inkuanen jacob ed pamilya to tan amin a kaiba to ibantak yo ray diriyos na arum a bansa ya awit yo linisan yoy sikayon dili insan kayo mampales na malinis onekal itayo la dia tan onla itayo ed betel a dimay panggawaan koy altar a para dios a tinmulong ed siak nen wala ak ed kairapan tan inoolup to ak ed inerman a nilak inter da sirin ed kinen jacob iray amin a walad sikaran diriyos na arum a bansa pati saray ikaw ya akabitin ed saray layag da inkotkot to ra yan amin ed silong na kiew a robli ya asingger ed sikem nen onsisiput si jacob tan saray anak ton lalaki sinmabiy baleg a takot ed saray totood kaliberliber iran baley kanyan ag da ra inosilan linmay jacob tan amin a totoo to diad luz a tatawagey betel natan diad dalin na canaan nanggawad man na altar tan inngaran to man a pasen na betel ta dimay pinayawaran na dios ed sikato nen ibabatikan toy agi to inatey si debora a nankomponid kinen rebeca nen ogaw ni tan imponpon dad silong na kiew a robli a walad abalaten na betel kanyan saman a kiew atawag na robli na ermen nen pinmawil si jacob a nanlapud mesopotamia pinmayawar lamet ed sikato so dios tan binindisionan to inkuan na dios ed sikato jacob so ngaran mo balet manlapud natan israel la kanyan israel so inngaran na dios ed sikato insan inkuan na dios ed sikato siak so dios a makapanyarinamin nawalaan kay amayamay ya anak manlapud sika ray bansa tan arari iter kod sikay dalin ya inter kod kindi abraham tan isaac tan iter ko met ed saray kabyangay boleg mo no andi ka lad bilay insan tinaynan lay dios si jacob diman ed samay pasen ya akitongtongay dios ed sikato angipaalagey si jacob na baton pakanudnunotan tan insaklang tod dios diad impangikalbo toy alak tan larak na oliba inngaran to na betel iman a pasen tinaynan nen jacob tan say pamilya to so betel et nen asingger la ra ed efrata sinmabiy panaon a pananak nen raquel et nanairapan ed pampapasakit to nen mapalaloy pampapasakit to inkuan na manamyanak ed sikato ag ka natatakot raquel sakey a laki lamet so anak mo balet ompapatey si raquel nen kuan lan naoyus so bilay to inngaran to na benoni may ogaw balet inngaran nen ama to na benjamin nen inatey si raquel imponpon dad gilig na dalan a mamaarap ed efrata a tatawagen natan na betlehem angyan diman si jacob na baton pakanudnunotan anggad natan sikato niy tanda na lobuk nen raquel intuloy nen jacob so impankurang to tan nankampo ed biek a dapag na tori ed eder nen manaayam si jacob ed saman a pasen inakdulan nen ruben si bilha sakey ed saray asawan inamung nen ama to nadngelan nen jacob et mapalaloy pasnuk to labinduan amin iray lalakin anak nen jacob sikara yay anak tod kinen lea ruben say pangulowan ya anak nen jacob simeon levi juda isacar tan zabulon diad kinen raquel jose tan benjamin diad kinen bilha ya aripen nen raquel dan tan neftali diad kinen zilpa ya aripen nen lea gad tan aser nianak ira yan amin ed mesopotamia binmisitay jacob ed kinen ama ton isaac diad namre ya asingger ed hebron tan nanayaman nen abraham tan isaac nambilay si isaac na sanlasus tan walomploy taon kanyan mataktakken la nen inatey imponpon na saray anak to a di esau tan jacob
sikara ya so kabyangay boleg nen esau a tatawagen met na edom inaasawa nen esau iray bibiin taga canaan si ada ya anak nen elon a heteo si oholibama ya anak nen ana a lakin anak nen zibeon a heveo si basemat ya anak nen ismael tan agi nen nebayot saraya so anak to si elifaz ed kinen ada si reuel ed kinen basemat di jeus jalam tan core ed kinen oholibama nianak ira yan amin ed canaan si esau tinaynan toy agi ton jacob tan linmad sananey a dalin kaiba to ray asawa to saray anak to amin a totoon walad pakaoley to saray ayayep to tan amin a kayaryan to ya atipon tod canaan tinmaynan lapud kulang lay taganon niiter na dalin a panaayaman da nen jacob dakerakel iray ayayep da kanyan ag la ra nayarin manayam ed sakey a pasen nanayam si esau ed kapokdulan na edom sikara yay kabyangay boleg nen esau a sengeg na boleg da ray edomita nananak si ada ya asawa nen esau na sakey a laki a si elifaz limaray lalakin anak nen elifaz di timan omar zefo gatam tan kenaz diad kinen timna a sananey ya asawa nen esau walay anak ton sakey a si amalec nananak si basemat ya asawa nen esau na sakey a laki a si reuel apatiray lalakin anak nen reuel di nahat zera sama tan miza nananak si oholibama ya asawa nen esau na taloran lalaki di jeus jalam tan core si oholibama et anak nen ana ya anak nen zibeon sikara yay tribu a say sengeg da et si esau si elifaz a pangulowan a lakin anak nen esau so sengeg na sarayan tribu teman omar zefo kenaz core gatam tan amalec say sengeg da ra yan amin a tribu et si ada ya asawa nen esau si reuel ya anak nen esau so sengeg na sarayan tribu nahat zera sama tan miza say sengeg da ra yan amin a tribu et si basemat ya asawa nen esau saraya so tribu a say sengeg da et si esau a say asawa to si oholibama ya anak nen ana jeus jalem tan core si esau so sengeg na amin da ra yan tribu saray onaan a totoon nanayam ed dalin na edom et nankapiga ran tribu tan say sengeg da saray onggendan a kabyangay boleg nen seir a horeo lotan sobal zibeon ana dison ezer tan disan si lotan so sengeg na saray boleg di hori tan heman si lotan et walay biin agi to a si timna si sobal so sengeg na saray boleg di alvan manahat ebal sefo tan onam duaray lalakin anak nen zibeon a di aya tan ana sikato ya may ana ya akalmo na saray ampetang a sobul diad kalawakan nen ipapastol to ray asno nen ama to si ana so ama nen dison a sengeg na saray boleg di hemdan esban itran tan keran wala met so biin anak nen ana a si oholibama si ezer so sengeg na saray boleg di bilhan zaavan tan acan si disan so sengeg na saray boleg di uz tan aran sikara yay tribu na horeo diad dalin na edom lotan sobal zibeon ana dison ezer tan disan kasakbayan a walay ari ed israel saraya so arari a nanoley ed dalin na edom bela ya anak nen beor a taga dinaba jobab ya anak nen zera a taga bosra husam a taga teman hadad ya anak nen bedad a taga avit tinalo to ray madianita diad bakal ed bansa na moab samla a taga masreca saul a taga rehobot a gilig na ilog baalhanan ya anak nen acbor hadad a taga pau si mehetabel so asawa to ya anak nen matred tan apo nen mezahab si esau so sengeg na sarayan tribu na edomita timna alva jetet oholibama ela pinon kenaz teman mibzar magdiel tan iram say pasen a panaayaman na balang sakey a tribu et ningaran met ed ngaran to man a tribu
nanayam si jacob diad dalin na canaan a nanayaman met nen ama to sikato yay istoria na pamilya nen jacob si jose a mantaoy labimpito so manaasikaso ed saray karniro tan kanding kaiba to ray agagi ton lalaki ya anak di bilha tan zilpa ya asawa met ira nen ama to indalem tod kinen ama to ray maoges a gagawaen da ray agagi to inararo nen jacob si jose nen saray arum ya anak to ta nianak nen masiken lay jacob inggawaan toy jose na kawes ya andokey so taklay to nen anengneng na saray agagi nen jose ya inaro ni nen jacob ya ama ra nen say sikara aliwaliway pitotongtong dad sikato lapud kabkabosul da aminsan a labi nankogip si jose et tinongtong to ya ed saray agagi to inkuanto dengel kayod kogip ko wala tayon amin ed kaalogan a mambeberber na trigo inmalagey imay binerber ko tan nantanyareg saray binerber yo et niliber da tan tinmuek ira anto abaloan mo sirin manari kad sikami tepet na saray agagi to kanyan lalon binosul da lapud saray imbagbaga ton nipaakar ed kogip to insan nankogip lamet si jose tan inkuantod saray agagi to nankogip ak lamet anengneng koy agew bulan tan labinsakey a bitewen a tinmuek irad siak imbaga to met yan kogip to ed kinen ama to et nampasnukan da anto tan a kogip inkuanen ama to abaloan mo sirin si inam saray agagim tan siak et ondago kamin ondakmomod sika mangimon iray agagi nen jose ed sikato balet ninudnunot ira ya nen ama to aminsan ya agew nen saray agagi nen jose et linma rad sikem a mampastol na saray karniro nen ama ra inkuanen jacob ed kinen jose laen mo ra may agagim dimad sikem a kawalaan dan pampapastolan inmebat si jose on ama inkuanen ama to nengneng mo no antoy kipapasen da ray agagim tan saray karniro insan pawil ka dia tan ibagam ed siak kanyan pinasiput nen ama to ed patar na hebron sinmabiy jose ed sikem tan manliliberliber diman nen anengneng na sakey a too a nantepet antoy aanapen mo aanapen ko ray agagik a mampapastol na karniro ebat to ibagam pad siak no iner so kawalaan da inkuanto may too andi la ra dia arengel kon ibabaga ra ya onla rad dotan kanyan tinombuk ira nen jose ed dotan et nalmo to rad man anengneng da nen arawi ni tan kasakbayan to ran naasinggeran nantotongtongan dan pateyen inkuan na sakey tan sakey ed sikara nia la may managkogip pateyen tayo insan tayo ibantak ed bobun so bangkay to ibaga tayon pinatey na ayep ed katakelan nengnengen tayod satan no antoy pagmaliwan na saray kogip to nadngel ira nen ruben kanyan labay ton iyagel si jose ag tayo ekalay bilay inkuanto ibantak yo labat ed sayay bobun diad kalawakan balet ag yo didiwiten inkuanto ya pian niagel tod sikara tan nipawil tod kinen ama to nen sinmabiy jose inekal day kawes ton andokey so taklay insan siningkat da tan imbuntok dad bobun a nakatan nen mangakan ira anengneng day olup na saray ismaelita a nanlapud galaad tan mamapaarap irad egipto napnoy beneg na kamilyo ra na pasas tan rikado inkuanen juda ed saray agagi to antoy nagunggona tayod pamatey ed agi tayo insan tayo ibori ilako ti lad saray ismaelita diad ontan ag ti la napasakitan agi tayo ni met kalamanan tan kadalaan tayo inmabubon ira may agagi to nen onlalabas iray komirsiantin madianita inagwat na saramay sanaagi si jose insan da inlakoy duamplon kuartan pilak ed saray ismaelita inawit da sirin si jose ed egipto nen pinmawil ed samay bobun si ruben tan anengneng ton anggapo lad may jose pinilat toy kawes to diad ermen to linmad saray agagi to tan inkuanto andid man si jose antoy gawaen ko amatey iray sakey a kanding tan insawsaw dad dala to so kawes nen jose inyakar da may kawes ed kinen ama ra tan inkuanda nalmo mi ya nengneng yo pa no kayaryan nen anak yo abirbir to tan inkuanto on kawes to pinatey na sakey ya ayep ed katakelan abingbingkas si jose ya anak ko pinilat nen jacob so kawes to diad ermen to tan nansolung na sako abayag a nanermen lapud si anak to dinmagon amin iray anak ton lalaki tan bibii a manligliwad sikato balet ag to labay so naligliwa tan inkuanto anggan wala ak lad pasen a panaayaman da ray inaatey panermenan ko ni so anak ko kanyan ag to tinondaan ya inermenan si anak ton jose leleg a nagagawa ra ya inlako na saramay madianita si jose ed kinen potifar diad egipto sakey ed saray opisyal na ari si potifar tan pangulo na saray guardia ed palasio
ag abayag nanlapud samay impangilakod jose tinaynan nen juda iray agagi to tan linmad kinen hira a taga baley na adullam akabat tod may sakey a biin cananea a say ama to et manngaray sua inasawa to nanlokun tan nananak na sakey a laki ya inngaran to na er nanlokun lamet tan nananak na sakey a laki ya inngaran to na onan nananak na kumatlon laki ya inngaran to na sela walad aczib si juda nen nianak si sela si juda inalaan toy er na asawa a tamar so ngaran to maoges so kagagawa nen er kanyan nampasnuk so katawan tan pinatey to inkuanen juda ed kinen onan ya agi nen er laka ta akdulan moy balo ya ayrom gawam so kanepegan mon agi na asawa to pian nawalaan na anak so agim balet amta nen onan ya ag nibilang iran anak to iray nailalak to kanyan kapag miakdul ed kinen ayro to iyibung tod dalin so bini to pian ag nawalaay anak si agi to nampasnuk so katawan ed sayan ginawa nen onan kanyan pinatey to met insan inkuanen juda ed kinen manugang to sempet ka nid abung nen amam tan ag ka ni miaasawa ya anggad ibaleg nen anak kon sela inkuanto ya lapud antakot ta ompan napatey met si sela a singa agawad saramay duaran agi to sinmempe la sirin si tamar ag abayag inatey so asawa nen juda nen asumpal so impanermen to linmad timna si juda tan si kaaro ton hira a taga adullam ed pasen a pankakatlian na saray karniro to walay angikuan ed kinen tamar onlay katolangan mo ed timna a mankatli na saray karniro to kanyan inekal toy kawes na balo ya akasolung ed sikato sinakbungan toy lupa to na pandung tan nanirung ed lolooban na enaim sakey a baley ed dalan a mamaarap ed timna kabat to a balolaki la si sela balet ag to ni inasaway tamar nen anengneng nen juda abaloan ton sakey a biin marotak ta sinakbungan toy lupa to inasinggeran tod gilig na dalan tan inkuanto gala ta paliket mo ak ag to amta a si tamar iman a manugang to inkuanto may bii antoy iter mod siak inmebat ipawitan ta kay kilaw na kanding inkuanto labay ko no itdan mo ak na kaletan ya anggad pakaawat koy kanding antoy iter kod sikan kaletan tepet nen juda inmebat say singsing mon panagmarka a pati say kadina to tan say baston a sankalibit mo inter ira sirin nen juda ed sikato nanakdul ira et nanlokun si tamar sinmempet lay tamar inekal toy pandung to tan insolung to lamet iray kawes na balo imbaki nen juda si kaaro ton hira a mangiter na samay kanding ya insipan to tan mangala na samay kaletan ya inter to balet ag naalmo nen hira imay bii tinepet tod pigaran lalaki ed enaim kawalaan to may biin marotak a wadya nen saman ed gilig na dalan inmebat ira anggapo pa ni dian balut so ontan a bii pinmawil ed kinen juda tan inkuanto ag ko naalmo inkuan na saray lalakid man ya anggapo nid man a balut so biin marotak inkuanen juda paolyan mo la sirin ya iyatol to ra may inter ko ta ompan elekan ita na saray totoo talagan bayaran ko met ingen et ag mo met naalmo kasumpal na sakey a taloy bulan walay angikuan ed kinen juda walay piaakdulan nen manugang mon si tamar ta malokun ingganggan nen juda ipaway yo insan yo poolan ya anggad ag to ipatey nen ipapaway da si tamar impaibaga tod kinen katolangan to alokunan ak na lakin akankayaryan ed saraya nengneng mo ra tan ibagam no siopay akankayaryansayan singsing a pati kadina to tan sayan baston abirbir ira nen juda tan inkuanto anggapoy kasalanan to ta ag ko ginaway kanepegan kod sikato impaasawak komun ed kinen anak kon sela ag lan balut inakdulan nen juda si tamar nen asingger lan mananak si tamar nalmoan a lasun a lalaki so iyanak to nen mampapasakit impaway na sakey ed sikara so lima to siningkat na manamyanak imay lima binerberan to na ambalangan tinebey tan inkuanto sikato yay onaan a pinmaway balet ginoyur na samay ogaw so lima to tan samay agi to la laingen so onaan a pinmaway insan inkuanto may manamyanak onya manaya so kapapaway mo kanyan angaranay fares sinmoblay a pinmaway so agi to samay walay ambalangan tinebey ed lima to et angaranay zara
saramay ismaelita inyakar dad egipto si jose tan inlako rad kinen potifar sakey ed saray opisyal na ari tan kapitan na saray guardiad palasio walad si jose sa katawan kanyan maaligwas so bilay to nanayam ed abung na amo ton egipsio anengneng na amo to a walad si jose so katawan tan maung so pansusumpalay amin a gagawaen to makaliliket ed sikato si potifar kanyan ginawa to a dilin aripen to impasen ton inkargado na abung to tan amin a kayaryan to nanlapud saman binindisionan na katawan so sankapamilyaan nen potifar lapud kinen jose binindisionan na katawan ya amin iray walad abung to tan ed siak so dala na agim singa bosis ya onkekerew na bales nisamba ka ag mo la nadalusan so dalin a singa inlokas toy sangi to nen inesep toy dala na agim a pinatey mo no ondalus ka anggapoy naanim magmaliw kan anggapoy abung tan akarakar ka diad tapew na dalin inkuanen cain ed katawan ambelat a tuloy yan dusa ag ko nasungdoan patataynanen mo ak ed dalin tan diad arap mo magmaliw ak ya anggapoy ag abayag nankasalanan ed ari so inkargadoy alak tan say pangulon panadiro ed palasio diad pasnuk na arid sikara impaipriso to rad abung na kapitan da ray guardia a diman met so akaiprisoan nen jose say dios so manangipatalus inkuanen jose ibaga yod siak ira tay kogip yo kanyan inkuanto may inkargadoy alak ed palasio diad kogip ko walay tanaman ya ubas ed arap ko a taloray sanga to kapaway na kogip ko sankaagtok so taloran pananginay tinapay diad samay pananginan a walad tapew wadman ya amin so klasiy kakanen a para ari balet totoktoken na saray manok inmebat si jose niay talus to saramay kalabas na duay taon kinogip na arid egipto a sikatoy manalalagey ed pandel na ilog na nilo kabebekta pinmaway ed ilog so pitoran baka a mararakep tan matataba tan nankakabkab ira na dika insan nanlapud kalawakan saramay pitoran dawa ya apa inakmun da ra may pitoran maiiyan aliing so ari tan naamtaan ton nankogip kaimbuas agunigon kanyan impaawit to ray amin a salamangkiro tan saray makabat sikato man a kupa so paniinoman to tan pampaparlesan to balbaleg a kaogsan so ginawa yo nen nabot ira na samay aripen inolit to ra man a salita inmebat ira antoy labay mon ibaga diad pansasalitam na ko tan saray arum nayarian da lay onla kanyan tampol ya inyabeba dad dalin iray sako ra insan da ra nilolokasan nananap a maung imay aripen nen jose pinalapu tod sankapangulowanan ya anggad sankayogtanan et nalmod sako nen benjamin imay kupa pinipilat na saramay sanaagi iray kawes da a pangipanengneng day ermen da impapawil da ra may sako ra ed beneg na saray asno ra insan ira pinmawil inmasingger si juda ed kinen jose tan inkuanto abuloyan mo ak pan misalitad sika ag ka komun mamapasnuk ed siak o katawan kaparam lay ari tinepet mod sikami no walay ama mi o agi mi inyebat min walay papaolyan ya ompatey anggapo lay kuarta mi inmebat si jose awit yo ra diay ayayep yo sikara lay ibayar yod tagano ya iter kod sikayo no anggapo lay kuarta yo kanyan inawit dad kinen jose iray ayayep dan kabayo karniro kanding baka tan asno diad saman a taon initdan to ray nakan a salat na saray ayayep da nen ontombuk a taon linma rad sikato tan inkuanda ag mi iyamut ed sika ya anggapo lay kuarta mi pati saray ayayep mi et kayaryan mo la ra anggapo lay nakdaan ya iter mid sika likud ed saray laman mi tan saray dalin mi ag mo kami papaolyan ya ompatey gawam so manepeg a polaing ag mo aabuloyan bini ya itanem mid kaalogan mi sinaliw nen jose a para ari so amin a dalin ed egipto apasootan ya amin iray egipsio a mangilakoy dalin da ta mapalaloy eras nagmaliw sirin a kayaryan na ari so amin a dalin manlapud sakey a samput ya anggad sananey a samput na egipto impagmaliw nen jose ya aripen iray totoo say dalin labat na saray papari so ag to sinaliw ag da kinaukolan ya ilako ray dalin da ta walay inter na ari a pambilay da inkuanen jose ed saray totoo sinaliw ta kayo la tan saray dalin yo a para ari niay trigo ya itanem yod kaalogan yo no panagani iter yoy kakalima ed ari say kera ikana yon bini tan tagano yo tan tagano na saray pamilya yo inmebat ira sinambot moy bilay mi tan maung kad sikami paaripen kami lad ari kanyan impaakseb nen jose so sakey a ganggan ed egipto a kayaryan na ari so kakalima na ani wala ni yan ganggan ya anggad natan saray dalin labat na papari so ag kayaryan na ari nanayam ed egipto ira may israelita diad gosen minmayaman ira tan dinmakerakel ira nanayam ag abayag ed samay impantongtong dan sanama nibagad kinen jose a mansasakit si ama to kanyan intagar to ray duaran lalakin anak to a di manases tan efraim ta nengnengen day jacob nen nibagad kinen inkuantod siak parakelen kon maung so kabyangay pamilyam pian magmaliw ya amayamay a bansa iray kabyangay boleg mo iter kod saray kabyangay boleg mo yan dalin tan kayaryanen da ed anggad angga intuloy ya inkuanen jacob ibibilang kon anak iray duaran lalakin anak mo a nianak ed egipto kasakbayan na inyakar ko dia anak ko ra di efraim tan manases a singa di ruben tan simeon no wala ni ray anak mon siopa ra yan ogogaw inmebat si jose anak ko ran inter na dios ed siak diad egipto inmebat si jacob iyasingger mo ra diad siak pian nabindisionan ko ra korarap la ray mata nen jacob lapud masiken la tan ngalngali la ag makanengneng inyasingger nen jose ira may ogogaw ed sikato nilakap to ra tan inanguban to ra inkuanen jacob ed kinen jose ag kon balut inilaloan a nanengneng ta ka ni et natan inyabuloy ni ingen na dios a nanengneng kon pati saray anak mo inala nen jose ira may ogogaw ed akwalan nen jacob tan dinmakmomon anggad dalin so lupa to inyan nen jose si efraim diad nikawigi nen jacob tan si manases diad nikawanan balet impankorusan nen jacob iray taklay to tan intapew tod olo nen efraim so kawanan a lima to anggaman a sikatoy yogtan tan say kawigin lima to diad tapew na olo nen manases a sikatoy pangulowan insan to binindisionan ni jose sarayan lalaki bindisionan ira komun na dios say dios a nilingkuran di amak ya abraham tan amak ya isaac bindisionan ira komun na dios ya angiwanwan ed siak ya anggad sayan agew bindisionan ira komun na anghil ya angipaliis ed siak ed antokaman a kaogsan mansiansia komun ed panamegley da so ngaran ko tan say ngaran di amak ya abraham tan amak ya isaac nawalaan ira komun na amayamay a kabyangay boleg agoloy isip nen jose nen anengneng ton intapew nen ama tod olo nen efraim so kawanan a lima to kanyan inala tod olo nen efraim so lima nen ama to ta iyalis tod olo nen manases inkuantod kinen ama to aliwan ontan ama sikato yay pangulowan itapew yod olo to so kawanan a lima yo ag inmabuloy si ama to tan kuanto on amtak anak ko magmaliw met a matalonggaring a totoo iray kabyangay boleg nen manases balet magmaliw a matalonggaring ni so yogtan to nen say sikato tan magmaliw a matalonan bansa iray kabyangay boleg to diad saman ya agew binindisionan to met ira may ogogaw a kuanto ikana na saray israelita so kangaranan yo diad pamindision da ikuanda pagmaliwen kayo komun na dios a singa di efraim tan manases diad onya insaginonur nen jacob si manases ed kinen efraim insan inkuanen jacob ed kinen jose onung na sankanengneng mo magano ak lan ompatey balet mansiansian kaibam so dios tan papawilen to kad dalin na saray atateng mo diad sika aliwan saray lalakin agagim so pangitdan ko na sikem say mataban dalin a sinamsam kod saray amorreo diad panamegley na ispadak tan panak
impaawit nen jacob iray anak ton lalaki tan kuanto gali diad abay ko ta ibagak so nagawad sikayo diad arapen a panaon mantitipon tan dengel kayo lalakin anak nen jacob dengel kayod ama yon israel ruben ya anak kon pangulowan sikay biskeg ko tan onaan ya anak ko nen kabisbiskegan ko say sankamapaatageyan tan sankabiskegan ed amin da ray anak kon lalaki singa ka mabiskeg a delap balet ag ka magmaliw a sankatalonggaringan lapud akiakdul kad inamung kon bii tan dinotakan moy dokulan na amam sanagi ra di simeon tan levi ikakana ray armas dad panggawa ray deral ag ak mibalid maamut iran to may manok balet ag to ilaus insan to ipool ya intiro ed tapew na altar makapaliket ed katawan so balingit na sayan bagat
di nadab tan abiu a lalakin anak nen aaron inala ra so pananginay insinso na balang sakey ed sikara kinargaan da ra na ngalab tinapewan da ra na insinso insan da ra inyapay ed katawan balet aliwa yan masanton apoy ta say katawan ag to ra ingganggan ya iyapay da kabebekta say katawan angipelag na apoy tan pinoolan to ra ya anggad ag da impatey ed arap to insan inkuanen moises ed kinen aaron sikato yay sasalitaen na katawan nen inkuanto amin da ray manlingkur ed siak nepeg a pagalangan day inkasantok ipatnag kod saray totook so kagalangan ko balet ag inmesel si aaron tinawag nen moises ira di misael tan elzafan a lalakin anak nen uziel a pangamaen nen aaron tan kuantod sikara gali dia ta alsa yo ray bangkay na kakapinsan yo diad masanton tulda tan iyakar yo rad paway na kampo kanyan dinmago ra tan say kawes ya akasolung ed saramay bangkay so nanlibitan da nen impaway da rad kampo onung na ingganggan nen moises insan inkuanen moises ed kinen aaron tan diad saray lalakin anak to a di eleazar tan itamar ag yo papaolyan ya agotgot so buek yo odino pipilaten iray kawes yo diad pangipanengneng yon maneermen kayo no gawaen yo ompatey kayo tan say katawan mampasnuk ed amin ya israelita balet amin a kapara yon israelita et naabuloyan iran manermen lapud sayan patey a say makasengeg et say apoy ya impelag na katawan ag kayo ontataynan ed lolooban na tulda ta no ontaynan kayo ompatey kayo lapud nisaklang kayo diad panamegley na ilalana a larak na katawan kanyan ginawa ra so imbaga nen moises say katawan kuantod kinen aaron sika tan saray lalakin anak mo et ag nepeg ya onloob ed tuldan ayaman ko kayari yon oninom na alak odino arum nin mabayanin inomen ta no gawaen yo ya ompatey kayo sikato ya so sakey a ganggan a nepeg a sumpalen na amin a kabyangay boleg mo nepeg yon pambiigan so bengatlan kayaryan na dios tan say bengatlan kayaryan na karaklan nepeg yo met a pambiigan so malinis tan say marotak onung ed ganggan nepeg yo met ya ibangat ed saray totood israel iray amin a ganggan ya inter kod sikara diad panamegley nen moises si moises inkuantod kinen aaron tan saray nakdaan a lalakin anak to a di eleazar tan itamar ala yoy bagat a trigo ya akeraan ed bagat a popoolan ed katawan gawa yon tinapay ya anggapoy libadura insan yo kanen ed abay na altar lapud masanton tuloy yan bagat akan yod sakey a masanton pasen sikato ya so betang yo tan saray lalakin anak yo ed bagat a popoolan ed katawan sikato ya so ingganggan ed siak na katawan balet sikayo tan saray anak yon lalaki tan bibii et nayarian yon kanen so pagew tan say kamanonur a sali a nisaklang a nidomadoman rigalo ed katawan a para saray papari nayarian yo ran kanen ed sakey a pasen a malinis onung ed ganggan sarayan bagat et niiter irad sikayo a parti ran nabebetangan yo ed saray bagat a para kareenan ya isaklang na saray totood israel awiten da so kamanonur a sali tan say pagew no isaklang a bagat a popoolan ed katawan so taba sarayan parti et kayaryan yo ra ed ando lan ando sikayo tan saray anak yo onung na ingganggan na katawan si moises tinepet to so nipaakar ed samay kanding ya ibagat para kasalanan et naamtaan to ya apoolan la lapud saya akapasnuk si moises ed kinen eleazar tan si itamar inkuantod sikara akin et ag yo inakan ed masanton pasen imay bagat a para kasalanan masanton tuloy iman et say katawan inter tod sikayo pian napaandi toy kasalanan na amin da ray israelita bangta say dala to et ag niakar ed dalem na masanton tulda nepeg komun ya inakan yod man imay bagat onung na ingganggan ko inmebat si aaron natad sayan agew say totoo angisaklang irad arap na katawan na bagat dan para kasalanan tan bagat a popoolan balet siansian makapasinagem so agawad siak no angan ak natan ed samay bagat a para kasalanan makapaliket ya kasi ed katawan akaliket si moises nen nadngel to yan ebat nen aaron
say katawan inter tod kindi moises tan aaron iray onggendan a totontonen a nepeg a tombuken na saray totood israel nayarian yon kanen so dinan man ya ayep ed tapew na dalin a pisag so koko to tan mamparintek balet ag yo nepeg a kanen iray kamilyo saray konihod takel odino saray konihon amo ipasen yon marotak ira yan ayayep ta mamparintek ira balet aliwan pisag so koko ra ag kayo mamangakan na baboy ta ipasen yon marotak ya ayep pisag iray koko to balet ag mamparintek ag kayo mamangakay dinan man ed sarayan ayayep ni didiwiten so laman ton inatey marotak ira yan ayayep nayarian yo a kanen so anggan dinan a sira a nanggigim tan nansiksik balet ag nayarin kanen so antokaman a manaayam ed danum ya anggapoy gigim tan siksik ipasen yon marotak ira yan sira ag yo ra kakanen ni didiwiten iray laman dan inatey ag kayo mamangakay antokaman a mabilay ya ag nansiksik tan ag nanggigim a manaayam ed danum ag yo nepeg a kanen iray onggendan a marotak a manok agila kulayot baga gikgik busardo buitri wawak abistrus garsita tigkalak dulakak pilikano kalamon abudilla tan kaging amin a nampayak a bigis et marotak likud labat ed saray manlukso nayarian yoy mangan na dorun dalokduk odino wirwir balet amin a nampayak tan mankorung et ipasen yo ran marotak siopamay makadiwit ed inatey a laman na saray onggendan ya ayayep et marotak ya anggad labi amin ya ayayep a nankoko likud no pisag so koko ra tan mamparintek ira tan amin ya ayayep ya apatiray sali tan andorokey so koko ra siopamay manawit na inatey a laman da ra yan ayayep nepeg ya ipesak toy kawes to balet sikatoy marotak ni ya anggad labi ipasen yon marotak iray bulilit otut tilay toko tiki buaya basakay tan angga siopamay maniwit ed saraya odino say inatey a laman da et marotak ya anggad labi amin a bengatlan adapoan na laman dan inatey et marotak sarayan bengatla et tabla abel katat odino sako ya anggan antoy pangikakanaan nakaukolan ya itaksaw irad danum balet mansiansia ran marotak ya anggad labi et no dinmapod banga so inatey a laman da amin a karga to may banga magmaliw a marotak tan nepeg yon betagen amin a kakanen a naibungan na danum a walad saman a banga et magmaliw a marotak tan amin a nayarin inumen a wadman ed saman a banga et magmaliw a marotak anggan anton bengatla a nadapoan na inatey a laman et magmaliw a marotak say dalin a dalikan odino pogun et nepeg a betagen balet say sobul odino bobun et mansiansian malinis anggaman ya amin a bengatlan nadiwit na inatey a laman et magmaliw a marotak no nadapoan day bokel ya itatanem samay bokel mansiansian malinis balet no say bokel ya akatalem ed danum et napelagan na inatey a laman na ayep a marotak samay bokel magmaliw a marotak siopamay makadiwit na inatey a laman na sakey a nayarin kanen et magmaliw a marotak ya anggad labi no walay mangan na anggan dinan a parti na samay inatey ya ayep nepeg ton ipesak so kawes to balet sikato niy marotak ya anggad labi siopamay manawit na inatey ya ayep nepeg ya ipesak toy kawes to balet sikato niy marotak ya anggad labi ag yo nepeg so mansira na dinan man ya ankekelag ya ayep a manaakar ed tapew na dalin ta marotak ira nayarin sarayan ayayep et maniilas ira odino panaakar day apatiran sali ra odino amayamay so sali ra ag yo dodotakay sikayon dili diad pangan yod sarayan ayayep siak so katawan a dios yo kanyan nepeg a masanto kayo ta siak et masanto ak siak so katawan ya angipaway ed sikayod egipto pian siak so magmaliw a dios yo nepeg a masanto kayo ta siak et masanto ak sikato ya sirin so ganggan a nipaakar ed saray ayayep tan saray manok nipaakar ed amin a manaayam ed danum tan amin a manaakar ed tapew na dalin apiger yon pambiigan so malinis tan say marotak onung ed ganggan saray ayayep a nayarin kanen tan saray ayayep a sebel a kanen
say katawan inter to ray onggendan a totontonen a nepeg a sumpalen na saray totood israel diad loob na pitoran agew kayariy pananak na sakey ya ina ed sakey a laki sayan ina et marotak onung ed ganggan a singa inkarotak to no naliliberan diad kumawalon agew nepeg a segaten so ogaw sayan ina talomplo tan taloy agew ni a siansian marotak lapud inkaekalan toy dala nen mananak nepeg ya ag to mandiwit na antokaman a masanto ni onloob ed dalem na masanton tulda ya anggad pagmaliw to lan malinis onung ed ganggan diad loob na labinapat agew kayariy pananak na ina ed sakey a bii sayan ina et marotak onung ed ganggan a singa inkarotak to no naliliberan insan anemaplo tan anem ya agew ni a siansian marotak lapud inkaekalan toy dala nen nananak no nagmaliw lan malinis onung ed ganggan kayari na inkarotak to lapud impananak to na laki odino bii nepeg a mangyakar ed pari diad lolooban na tuldan ayamay katawan na sakey taon a kordiro ta isaklang a bagat a popoolan tan say sakey a malapati odino sakey a palekpek ta isaklang a bagat a para kasalanan say pari isaklang to yan bagat ed katawan tan gawaen toy sirimonya a mangekal na inkarotak to et diad ontan magmaliw a malinis onung ed ganggan sikato ya sirin so nepeg a gawaen na sakey a bii kayari ton mananak no ag nayarian na sakey a bii so mangibagat na sakey a kordiro nepeg a mangisaklang na duaran palekpek odino duaran malapati say sakey isaklang a bagat a popoolan tan say sakey ibagat a para kasalanan say pari gawaen toy sirimonya a mangekal na inkarotak na samay bii et diad ontan magmaliw a malinis onung ed ganggan
say katawan inter tod kindi moises tan aaron ira yan totontonen no say sakey a too et agiri odino apelsaan odino alanokan a nayarin magmaliw a singa sakit a kating iyakar ed kinen aaron odino diad sakey ed saray paparin anak to say pari nengnengen to may sakit na baog et no pinmoti ray bagod kawalaan to tan singa kinmotlaung singa kating yan sakit say pari ed satan sintinsiaan ton marotak imay too balet no samay sakit na baog et ampoti tan ag kinmotlaung tan ag pinmoti ray bago say pari panayamen ton pitoy agew a bukbukor to imay too ed akabiig a pasen say pari nengnengen to lamet diad kumapiton agew imay too no diad pakanengneng to et ag angoman imay sakit tan ag kinmayat panayamen to nin pitoy agew ed akabiig a pasen samay pari nengnengen to lamet diad kumapiton agew et no nakal so poti to may sakit tan ag kinmayat sintinsiaan ton malinis imay too onung ed ganggan sakey labat a giri samey too ipesak tok kawes to et magmaliw a malinis onung ed ganggan balet no samay sakit et kinmayat kayari na impannengneng tan impanintinsia na pari a malinis imay too nepeg a mampanengneng lamet imay too ed pari say pari nengnengen to lamet et no kinmayat imay sakit sintinsiaan to a marotak imay too kating so sakit to no say sakey a too et walay sakit ton kating iyakar ed pari a mannengneng ed sakit na samay too no walay ampotin babag ed baog to ya amapoti na saray bago tan pinmaway lay laman saya et abayag lan kating say pari sintinsiaan ton marotak ag la nakaukolan a papawilen ton panayamen ed samay akabiig a pasen mapatpatnag lan sikatoy marotak no samay sakit et onkayat ed intiron laman to manlapud olo ya anggad sali to say pari nengnengen to lamet no narumog ton kinmayat ed intiron laman to sintinsiaan ton malinis onung ed ganggan no amin a baog to et nagmaliw ya ampoti sikato so malinis onung ed ganggan balet manlapud bekta a walay tinmerak a babag sikato so marotak say pari nengnengen to lamet tan no nanengneng to so tinmerak a babag sintinsiaan ton marotak imay too say tinmerak a babag et sakey a sakit a kating kanyan marotak imay too balet no onabig so babag a tinmerak tan nagmaliw ya ampoti lamet samay too onla ed pari a mannengneng lamet ed sikato et no pinmoti imay sakit sikatoy malinis onung ed ganggan tan say pari sintinsiaan ton malinis no say sakey a too et walay pelsa ton inmabig la balet no ag abayag et walay linmetaw ya ampotin larag odino ampotin balangaan a batek ed nanlapwan na samay pelsa sikatoy onla ed pari nengnengen na pari et no kinmotlaung imay batek tan pinapoti to ray bago sintinsiaan ton marotak kating yan sakit a ginmapod pelsa balet no say pari et nengnengen to may batek tan narumog ton ag pinmoti rad may bago tan ag kinmotlaung balet ta posisawan so kolor to say pari panayamen ton pitoy agew imay mansasakit ed akabiig a pasen no onkayat imay batek say pari sintinsiaan ton marotak walay sakit to balet no anggapoy pangomanan to may batek tan ag onkayat sakey labat a piglat na pelsa tan say pari sintinsiaan ton malinis imay too onung ed ganggan no say sakey a too et apoolay parti na laman to tan nagmaliw ya ampoti odino ampotin balangaan a batek so apoolan a laman say pari nengnengen to no pinmoti ray bago diad kawalaay batek tan kinmotlaung kating yan sakit a ginmapod inpakapoolan to sintinsiaan ton marotak balet no ag pinmoti ray bago diad apoolan a parti tan ag kinmotlaung balet ta posisawan so kolor to say pari panayamen ton pitoy agew a bukbukor to imay too ed akabiig a pasen say pari nengnengen to lamet diad kumapiton agew et no onkakayat imay batek talagan sakit a kating tan say pari sintinsiaan ton marotak imay too balet no anggapoy angomanan to may batek tan ag onkakayat tan posisawan so kolor to aliwan sakit a kating say pari sintinsiaan ton malinis imay too onung ed ganggan lapud sakey labat a piglat na samay apoolan no say sakey a laki odino say sakey a bii et walay sakit tod baog na olo odino baba say pari nengnengen to may sakit no singa kinmotlaung tan saray bagod samay kawalaay sakit et duyawan tan pino kating yan sakit say pari sintinsiaan tod satan a marotak imay too no diad pannengneng na pari ed samay too et naalmoan ton ag kinmotlaung imay sakit balet ta aliwa nin magket iray bago panayamen to na pitoy agew a bukbukor to may too ed akabiig a pasen diad kumapiton agew say pari nengnengen to lamet imay sakit et no ag kinmayat tan anggapo ray duyawan a bago ed kawalaay sakit tan ag kinmotlaung samay too kiskisan toy kaliberliber na samay sakit say pari ed satan panayamen to lamet na pitoy agew a bukbukor to imay too ed akabiig a pasen diad kumapiton agew say pari nengnengen to lamet imay sakit ta no ag kinmayat tan ag kinmotlaung sintinsiaan ton malinis imay too onung ed ganggan samay too ipesak toy kawes to tan sikatoy malinis la balet no kinmayat imay sakit kayari na impanintinsia ed sikato a malinis say pari nengnengen to lamet no kinmayat la so sakit ag to la nakaukolan a nengnengen no wala kasi odino anggapo so duyawan a bago mapatnag a samay too et marotak balet no diad pakanengneng na samay pari et ag kinmayat imay sakit tan totobuan la ra na magket a bago imay sakit inmabig lan talaga tan samay pari sintinsiaan ton malinis onung ed ganggan no say sakey a laki odino bii et wala ray ampotin batek ed baog to say pari nengnengen to yan too no ampotin posisaw so kolor na saray batek batek ira labat a linmetaw ed baog say too et malinis onung ed ganggan no say sakey a too et ayangyangan ed beneg na olo to odino diad arap na olo to sikatoy aliwan marotak no ag ta yangyangan labat balet no walay onletaw a balangaan ya ampotin giri ed samay ayangyangan a parti sakit yan kating say pari nengnengen to tan no walan talagay balangaan ya ampotin giri samay pari sintinsiaan ton marotak imay too lapud samay kating a walad olo to say toon walay kating ed laman to nepeg a mankawes na apilatpilat ag mansagaysay sakuban toy kapalduan lupa to ed bandad leksab tan oneyag marotak marotak mansiansian marotak legan a walay sakit to tan nepeg a manayam ya arawid saray totoo diad paway na kampo no walay boot ed kawes a lana odino linen odino boot ed abel a lana odino linen odino boot ed katat odino diad antokaman a ginawad katat no birdian odino balangaan so kolor to boot yan onkayat tan nepeg ya ipanengneng ed pari say pari nengnengen to tan isinup to na pitoy agew imay nipanengneng a bengatla nengnengen to lamet diad kumapiton agew et no kinmayat imay boot samay bengatla et marotak say pari poolan to lapud onkayat yan pikas a nepeg a deralen diad panamegley na apoy balet no diad panengneng na pari ed samay boot et narumog ton ag onkakayat ed samay bengatla iganggan to a nipesak tan nisinup nin pitoy agew insan to lamet nengnengen et no ag angoman so kolor na samay boot anggaman ya ag kinmayat siansia nin marotak nepeg yon poolan imay bengatla anggan say boot et walad arap odino diad beneg balet no diad pannengneng lamet na pari et kinmopas imay boot satsaten toy parti na kawes odino katat a kawalaay boot insan to ekalen insan no ompatnag lamet so boot onkakayat lamet tan nepeg a poolan na akankien so kawes odino katat no ipesak to et nakal imay boot ipesak to lamet et magmaliw lan malinis onung ed ganggan sikato ya sirin so ganggan a nipaakar ed boot ed kawes a lana odino linen o abel a lana odino linen odino diad pikas ed antokaman a ginawad katat
say katawan inter tod kinen moises iray onggendan a totontonen a nipaakar ed sirimonya a panlinis ed sakey a toon inmabig ed sakit a kating diad agew a say sakey a too et nasintinsiaan a malinis onung ed ganggan sikatoy niakar ed pari insan say pari iyakar tod paway na kampo tan diman to nengnengen no inmabig la may sakit say pari iganggan to a niakar ed sikato so duaran manok a malinis onung ed ganggan sakey a poter na kiew a sidro sakey ya ambalangan koldon tan sakey a sangay isopo insan say pari iganggan to a samay sakey a manok et pateyen ya akasalur so sakey a bangan nankarga na danum ya inalad sobol alaen to may sananey a manok tan isawsaw tod dala na samay pinatey a manok isawsaw to met imay kiew a sidro samay ambalangan koldon tan samay sangay isopo iwalsik ton mamimpito imay dala ed samay toon linisan ed sakit ton kating insan sintinsiaan ton malinis onung ed ganggan paibolus tod kaalogan imay mabilay a manok samay too ipesak toy kawes to poklisan toy olo to tan manames diad onya magmaliw a malinis onung ed ganggan nayarian toy onloob ed kampo balet ta manayam ni na pitoy agew ed paway na tulda to diad kumapiton agew kiskisan toy buek to balbas to kirep to tan amin a bagoy laman to ipesak toy kawes to tan manames diad onya magmaliw lan malinis onung ed ganggan diad kumawalon agew sikatoy mangyakar na laman a duaran kordiron kalakyan tan sakey a kordiron kabatyan a sakey taon ya anggapoy deral na laman da duaran kilon arina ya inkames ed larak na oliba tan talora tan kapalduan litro a larak na oliba say pari iyakar to may too tan sarayan bagat diad lolooban na tuldan ayamay katawan insan say pari alaen to may sakey a kordiron kalakyan tan katekep na samay taloran tan kapalduan litron larak isaklang to a bagat a pambayar isaklang to a nidomadoman rigalod katawan a para pari pateyen to may kordiro diad masanton pasen a panamateyan ed saray ayep ya ibagat para kasalanan tan saray ayep ya ibagat a popoolan nepeg to yan gawaen lapud say bagat a pambayar kawanan a lima to tan iwalsik tod man a mamimpito diad arapan na katawan mangala na daiset a larak a walad daklap to tan daiset a dala to may kordiro insan iporanis to rad kawanan a gilig na layag to sirimonya na panlinis insan say pari isaklang toy bagat a para kasalanan tan gawaen toy sirimonya na panlinis kayari to ya pateyen toy ayep a para bagat a popoolan tan katekep na bagat a trigo isaklang tod tapew na altar diad onya say pari gawaen toy sirimonya na panlinis tan samay too et magmaliw a malinis onung ed ganggan no mairap so bilay na sakey a too tan ag to nayarian ira yan ibagat mangyakar na sakey labat a kordiron kalakyan ya isaklang ton bagat a pambayar ya onkanan panlinis ed sikato onung ed ganggan sakey a nidomadoman bagat ed katawan a para pari sikatoy mangyakar na sakey labat a kilon arina ya inkames ed larak na oliba a para bagat a trigo tan talora tan kapalduan litron larak na oliba mangyakar met na duaran palekpek odino duaran malangwer a malapati say sakey ibagat katawan mangipoyuk na daiset a larak ed saramay pasen ya angiponarisan to na dala diad gilig na kawanan a layag to may too diad tangan na kawanan a lima to tan diad tangan na kawanan a sali to say akeraan ed samay larak a walad daklap to et ipoyuk tod olo na samay too tan diad onya gawaen to so sirimonya na panlinis insan mangisaklang na sakey ed saramay palekpek odino malangwer a malapati a sakey a bagat a para kasalanan tan say sananey para bagat a popoolan a katekep toy bagat a trigo diad onya say pari gawaen toy sirimonya na panlinis sikato ya so ganggan a sumpalen na toon walay sakit ton kating balet ag to nayarian ya isaklang so ingganan bagat a para panlinis to say katawan inter tod kinen moises tan aaron iray onggendan a totontonen a nipaakar ed saray abung a nabobootan sarayan totontonen et tombuken ira no saray totood israel et akaloob la ra ed dalin na canaan ya iter na katawan ed sikara siopamay makalmo na boot ed abung to nepeg ya ibaga tod pari say pari iganggan to ya ya anggad ompatey siopamay mamatey na kapara ton too nepeg a pateyen tan siopamay mamatey na ayep na kapara ton too nepeg a salatan to say bilay bayaran na bilay no sinugatan na sakey a too so kapara ton too nepeg a gawaen ed sikato so ginawa to no amoter na pokel na kapara ton too nepeg a poteren met so pokel to no anokit na mata na kapara ton too nepeg a sukiten met so mata to no angekal na ngipen na kapara ton too nepeg ya ekalen met so ngipen to no anugat na kapara ton too nepeg a sugaten met a singa impanugat to siopamay amatey na ayep na kapara ton too nepeg a salatan to balet aanien iray trigon tinmubon bukor tan ag yo boborboren so bunga na saray kaubasan ya ag yo pinotutan so wakawakal da sikatoy taon a pampainawan sigput na dalin anggaman ya ag adalusan so dalin ed katawan pian mambilay kayon arawid kaatapan ed dalin a panayaman yo say dalin mangiter na bunga to tan nawalaan kayo na amin a labay yon kanen tan mambilay kayod man ya arawid kaatapan nayarin walay mantepet no antoy pambilay yo legan na kumapiton taon ag taneman iray kaalogan tan ag borboren iray bungay tanaman say katawan bindisionan toy dalin diad kumanem a taon pian magenap a pambilay a duay taon so iter ton tagano no mantanem kayod kaalogan yo no kumawalon taon say pambibilay yo nid satan say naani yo ed kumanem a taon tan duga nin pambilay yo ya anggad pakaani yo lad intanem yo say dalin ag nepeg ya ilakon anggad angga lapud ag yo kayaryan say dios so akankayaryan tan singa kayo sangkailin naabuloyan a mangikana ed dalin no alako so dalin nepeg a birbiren so kanepegan na gendat pangaabangen ingen toluk yoy dios tan abuloyan yon manayam ed abay yo so kapara yon israelita ag yo pangaabangen ed kuartan ipabayes yod sikato tan ag yo panotoboan ed kakanen ya ilako yod sikato ira may kakanen a walad lima ra intapew to rad bagat a popoolan insan to ra pinaoolan ed tapew na altar sikato yay bagat a panangikonsagra sikato yay bagat a popoolan tan makapaliket ed katawan so balingit to insan inala nen moises so pagew tan inyapay ton sakey a nidomadoman rigalo ed katawan sikato yay parti a kayaryan nen moises ed samay karniron inkanad impangonsagra ginawa nen moises so onung na ingganggan na katawan inala nen moises imay larak ya ipopoyuk tan angala na daiset a dala a walad tapew na altar tan inwalsik tod kinen aaron tan diad saramay anak to winalsikan to met iray kawes da diad onya inkonsagra to rad katawan pati saray kawes da inkuanen moises ed kinen aaron tan saray anak ko iyakar yod lolooban na tuldan ayamay katawan so karni lambung yo tan akan yod aman a pati say tinapay a walad baskit na saray bagat na panangikonsagra onung na ingganggan na katawan poolan yoy amin a nakeraan a karni tan tinapay diad loob na pitoran agew ag kayo ontataynan ed lolooban na tulda ya anggad nasumpal so sirimonyay panangikonsagra ingganggan na katawan so ginawa tayo natan pian naekal so kasalanan yo diad loob na pitoran agew nepeg a manayam kayod mad lolooban na tulda diad agew tan labi tan gawa yoy ingganggan na katawan no ag yo sumpalen ompatey kayo sikato ya so ingganggan na katawan ed siak kanyan si aaron tan saramay anak to sinumpal day amin ya ganggan na katawan diad panamegley nen moises
diad ontombuk ya agew kayari na samay sirimonya na panangikonsagra si moises tinawag toy aaron tan saray anak ton lalaki tan saray pangulo na israel inkuantod kinen aaron mangala ka na sakey a kilaw na bakan kalakyan tan sakey a kordiron kalakyan ya anggapoy deral na laman da tan ibagat mo ra ed katawan say baka bagat a para kasalanan tan say kordiro bagat a popoolan insan ibagam ed saray totood israel a mangala ray sakey a kanding a kalakyan ta ibagat da a para kasalanan sakey taon a baka tan sakey taon a kordiro ya anggapoy deral na laman da ta isaklang da ran bagat a popoolan tan sakey a bakan kalakyan tan sakey a kordiron kalakyan ta ibagat da ran para kareenan ibagat da ra ya ed katawan a katekep da so bagat a trigo ya inkames ed larak nepeg da yan gawaen ta say katawan mampanengneng ed sikara natan inyakar dad arap na tulda ira may amin ya ingganggan nen moises ya awiten da tan nantitipon diman iray amin ya israelita ta igalang da so katawan inkuanen moises ingganggan na katawan a gawaen yo ra yan amin pian nipanengneng ed sikato so kagalangan to insan to inkuan ed kinen aaron lakad altar ta isaklang mo so bagat a para kasalanan tay say bagat a popoolan a mangekal na saray kasalanan mo tan saray kasalanan na saray totoo isaklang mo yan bagat a mangekal na saray kasalanan na saray totoo onung na ingganggan na katawan linmad altar si aaron tan pinatey to may kilaw na bakan kalakyan ta isaklang a bagat a para saray kasalanan to saramay anak to inyakar dad sikato so dala indelnet tod samay dala so tamoro to pinoranisan to may pinagkasaklur ed saray suyok na altar tan inibung tod leksab na altar so keran dala insan to pinoolan ed tapew na altar so taba saray batuk tan say sankaabigan a parti na altey onung na ingganggan na katawan ed kinen moises balet pinoolan tod paway na kampo so karni tan say katat na samay ayep pinatey to may ayep ya ikanad bagat a popoolan a para sikaton dili saramay anak to inyakar dad sikato so dala tan insibu ton amin ed saray apatiran dapag na altar inter dad sikato so olo tan saray arum a tegteg na samay ayep insan to ra pinoolan ed tapew na altar inorasan to ray loobloob tan saray kamanonur a sali intapew to rad saray arum a kabyangan na samay bagat a popoolan insan to ra pinoolan ed tapew na altar kayari to ya insaklang to ra may bagat na saray totoo inala to may kanding ya ibagat a para saray kasalanan da ray totoo pinatey to tan imbagat to a singa ginawa to ed samay bagat a pangekal na saray kasalanan to inala to met imay ayep para bagat a popoolan tan insaklang to onung ed saray totontonen inyapay to may bagat a trigo angala na sankaakup ya arina tan pinoolan tod tapew na altar kaaruman ya na inagewagew a bagat a popoolan pinatey to may bakan kalakyan tan samay karniron kalakyan ta ibagat ira a para kareenan sakey yan bagat a para saray totoo saramay anak ton lalaki inyakar dad sikato so dala tan insibo to ed apatiran dapag na altar si aaron intapew tod saray pagew na samay baka tan samay karniro iray taba say mataban ikol say taban kinmulyaput ed saray loobloob saray batuk tan say sankaabigan a parti na altey insan to ra inyakar ya amin ed altar pinoolan tod tapew na altar iray taba tan inyapay ton nidomadoman rigalod katawan a para saray papari ira so pagew tan saray kamanonur a sali onung na ingganggan nen moises nen asumpal nen aaron ya insaklang iray amin a bagat inyatagey to ray lima to tan impaarap to rad katoowan tan binindisionan to ra insan linmasur si moises tan si aaron linmoob irad dalem na samay tuldan ayamay katawan nen pinmaway ira binindisionan da ray katoowan tan pinmatnag ed amin a totoo so kagalangan na katawan kabebekta say katawan angipelag na apoy tan inoput ton pinoolan imay bagat a popoolan tan saramay taba ed tapew na altar nen anengneng ya na saray totoo inmeyag iran amin tan dinmakmomo ra ya anggad dalin
